# 获取当前路径下所有的 .lib 文件
set lib_files [glob *.lib]
rf64x64_tt_typical_0p90v_0p90v_85c.lib rf64x64_ssg_cworstt_0p81v_0p81v_125c.lib rf64x64_ffg_cbestt_0p99v_0p99v_m40c.lib
foreach lib $lib_files {
    read_lib $lib
        set current_lib [file rootname $lib]
    write_lib -format db $current_lib -output $current_lib.db
    remove_lib $current_lib
}
